1VPO      (VPO2193) (13:00) (15MAR04) WYLBUR'S VTAM PROGRAM OPERATOR                                                        Page    4
0Current Usings:  (CP,R11) (CV,R12)
0Loc    Object Code    Addr1 Addr2  Stmt Lv Lineno    Source Statement           (Hibal 5, Asmedit 3.3)  HLASM R4.0  2004/03/15 13.00
+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   1216              * THIS MODULE ALLOWS A WYLBUR USER TO ISSUE VTAM COMMANDS, AND
                                    1217              * TO RECEIVE THE REPLIES.
                                    1218              *
                                    1219              * THE CORRESPONDENCE BETWEEN THE WYLBUR COMMAND AND THE VTAM
                                    1220              * COMMAND IS AS FOLLOWS:
                                    1221              *
                                    1222              *            WYLBUR                          VTAM
                                    1223              *
                                    1224              *      [DUMP] VTAM D [NET] anything       D NET,anything
                                    1225              *      [DUMP] VTAM V [NET] anything       V NET,anything
                                    1226              *      [DUMP] VTAM F [NET] anything       F NET,anything
                                    1227              *
                                    1228              * Where "anything" is passed to VTAM unchanged, except that BLANKs
                                    1229              * and COMMAs as a WYLBUR separator are changed to a single COMMA,
                                    1230              * and the WYLBUR terminator (SEMI-COLON) ends the message.
                                    1231              *
                                    1232              * If a user includes the ",TEST=YES" parameter, it must be at
                                    1233              * the end of his command.
                                    1234              *
                                    1235              * The VTAM Application Name is taken from CVWYLSSN.  It must be
                                    1236              * authorized as a "Secondary Program Operator" in the VTAMLST dataset.
                                    1237              *
                                    1238              * A representative APPL definition statement is:
                                    1239              *
                                    1240              *        WYLBUR   APPL  AUTH=SPO,EAS=1
                                    1241              *
-                                   1243              * ORGANIZATION:
0                                   1245              * The MAIN TASK (WYLBUR) receives a command from a user, and
                                    1246              * validates that the user is authorized to make the command.
                                    1247              * A free slot in the fixed length User List is obtained,
                                    1248              * and the command to VTAM is placed in the Outbound Message Q.
0                                   1250              * Messages on the User Inbound Q are typed to the user.
0                                   1252              * The SUB-TASK (higher priority) handles all communication with VTAM.
                                    1253              * The ACB is opened if necessary.  Two RPLs are used, one outbound,
                                    1254              * and one inbound.  Requests are sent to VTAM, when found on the
                                    1255              * Outbound Message Q. Inbound messages are placed on the appropriate
                                    1256              * User's Inbound Message Q.
                                    1257              *
                                    1258              * When detecting the "VTCFWCLS" flag, the sub-task will close the
                                    1259              * ACB and terminate.
